"short-container-title": ["Parasitology"], "published-print": {"date-parts": [[1999, 10]]}, "abstract": "<jats:p>Genome projects for the parasitic helminths <jats:italic>Brugia malayi</jats:italic> (a representative filarial nematode) and <jats:italic>Schistosoma</jats:italic> were \ninitiated in 1995 by the World Health Organization with the ultimate objectives of identifying new vaccine candidates and \ndrug targets and of developing low resolution genome maps. Because no genetic maps are available, and very few genes \nhave been characterized from either parasite group, the first goal of both Initiatives has been to catalogue new genes for \nfuture placement on chromosome and physical maps. These genes have been identified by the expressed sequence tag \n(EST) approach, utilising cDNA libraries constructed from diverse life cycle stages. To date, the Initiatives have deposited \nover 16000 <jats:italic>Brugia</jats:italic> ESTs and nearly 8000 <jats:italic>Schistosoma</jats:italic> ESTs in Genbank's dbEST database, corresponding to 6000 and \nover 3600 genes respectively (33% of <jats:italic>Brugia</jats:italic>'s estimated gene compliment, 18\u201324% of that of <jats:italic>Schistosoma</jats:italic>). Large \nfragment, genomic libraries have been constructed in BAC and YAC vectors for studies of genomic organization and for \nphysical and chromosome mapping, and public, hypertext genomic databases have been established to facilitate data access. \nWe present a summary of progress within the helminth genome initiatives and give several examples of important gene \ndiscoveries and future applications of these data.</jats:p>", "DOI": "10.1017/s0031182099004473", "type": "journal-article", "created": {"date-parts": [[2002, 7, 27]], "date-time": "2002-07-27T13:30:22Z", "timestamp": 1027776622000}, "page": "19-38", "source": "Crossref", "is-referenced-by-count": 34, "title": ["Helminth genome analysis: the current status of the filarial \nand schistosome genome projects"], "prefix": "10.1017", "volume": "118", "author": [{"given": "S.
